  • HTML5 版本的更改列表
    • HTML5 version is now supported in the Firefox browser.
    • 修复了战斗中的分数栏，可获得无限分数或没有时间限制。
    • 翻译和用户界面的更改。
    • Added 展示 to the 商店 in the HTML5 version and Android version.
    • 使用旧版 HTML5 客户端的玩家现在会被重定向到新版 HTML5 版本。
    • Added 阴影 on 坦克 tracks.
    • 在过时和慢速的电脑上性能得到提升
    • 道具箱子动感区域 are no longer darkened on 夜晚模式地图.
    • 已将新闻添加到通讯工具中。


October 31 (Update 577)

  • 过速装置的变化：
    • 猛犸象's 过速装置:
      • 已移除无敌状态；
      • 已移除忽略物理影响；
      • 将持续时间从5秒增加到7秒；
      • 速度提升从30%增加到40%;
      • 已添加即时修复；
      • Added instant removal of 冷冻 and 着火 effects;
      • Cannot be disabled by 黄蜂轻甲's 过速装置.
    • 猎人中甲's 过速装置:
      • Decreased effect 半径 from 30 to 25 meters;
      • Decreased 持续时间 time from 3 to 2.7 seconds;
      • Increased delay before activation time from 1 to 1.1 seconds.
    • 黄蜂轻甲's 过速装置:
      • Doesn't disable 猛犸象's 过速装置 anymore.
  • 变更中的更改：
    • 冰风暴的变化 «震动冻结»:
      • Decreased 伤害 penalty from 50% to 30%;
      • 冷冻 rate increased from +100% to +200%.
    • 火箭炮’s alteration «Missile launcher “猎人中甲”»:
      • Removed 最高 projectile 速度 penalty.
    • 火箭炮的改装«导弹发射器“旋风”»：
      • Decreased 瞄准 time penalty from 40% to 30%.
    • 火箭炮的改造 «导弹发射器 “轴”»：
      • 投射物数量从4减少到2。
    • 火箭炮’s alteration «远程火箭炸药»:
      • 增加了最大弹丸速度限制为350米/秒。
    • 极速炮的改动 «更快速的水平跟踪»:
      • Decreased vertical auto-aim penalty from 30% to 15%.
    • 极速炮的改装 «射击速度调节器»:
      • Decreased 每秒伤害 from 20% to 15%.
  • Changes in the new HTML5 version:
    • Added remapping 控制 function;
    • Added WebGL1 support;
    • UI changes.

    • 镭射炮’s alteration «重型电容器»:
      • 将完整炮弹重装时间从 8 秒减少到 6 秒。

      • 将完整炮弹重装时间从2.5秒减少到2秒；

    • 剑圣:
      • If a 剑圣 self-destroys, 分数 points are given to the opponent. Previously they were deducted from your 团队’s 分数.

July 18 (Update 564)

  • Changes in the balance of 炮塔 and 过速装置:
  • 电磁炮:
    • Increased 瞄准 recovery time from 1 second to 2 seconds.
  • 冰风暴:
    • 全气缸排放时间从7秒减少到6.5秒。
  • "等离子焰炬” Alteration for 火龙珠:
    • Now reduces the 速度 of projectiles by 50% instead of 66%.
  • “狂暴” Alteration for 火龙珠:
    • 现在将射击的启动加速度提高30%，而不是80%。

    • Now reduces 炮塔 rotation 速度 by 30% instead of 70%.
  • 滑膛炮的“龙之吐息”改造：
    • Now each 颗粒 heats the target by 0.3% instead of 0.2%.
  • “高容量弹鼓” Alteration for 滑膛炮:
    • Now increases 弹匣炮弹重装时间 by 15% instead of 35%.
    • Now does not affect the 冷却 of shots in the clip.
  • “电子偶” Alteration for 滑膛炮:
    • Now increases clip 炮弹重装时间 by 15% instead of 10%.
  • “自适应重载” Alteration for 滑膛炮:
    • 现在，摧毁敌方坦克会完全重新装填弹夹。
  • 独裁者's 过速装置道具 activation effect:
    • 射程从15米增加到20米。
  • 守卫者无人机:
    • The effect 持续时间 is fixed at 20 seconds.
    • Increased 冷却 from 10 seconds to 20 seconds.
    • Reduced additional 启动加速度道具 with +(100-300)% to +(50-200)%.
  • 助推器无人机:
    • 效果持续时间固定为3秒。
    • Reduced 冷却 from 10 seconds to 3 seconds.
  • Changes in 匹配地图:
    • Removed 突袭模式 from 黑色森林地图.
    • 在死亡混战、团队对战、控制点模式中新增了一个实验性地图“群岛”。
    • Added 火车站 in 死亡混战, 团队对战, 控制点, 互夺军旗, 橄榄球, 突袭模式.
    • Added 十字路口地图 in 死亡混战, 团队对战, 控制点, 互夺军旗, 橄榄球模式.
    • 对不同地图的小修正。
  • 其他 changes:
    • Added “猫头鹰” 模块 to the "Anti-露营者" 防护模块套件
    • Added 48 hours to the July 星级挑战 and 战争 for 宇宙 to make up for starting them late.

    • 将所有改装的枪管旋转时间减少了 0.5 秒
  • 极速炮’s "燃烧带":
    • Now reduces 每秒伤害 by 20% instead of 10%
  • 极速炮的“射击速度调节器”
    • 现在将每秒伤害减少20%，而不是25%
  • 火箭炮’s Missile launcher "猎人中甲":
    • Reduced recharge time after volley:
      • M0：2.5 → 1.5；
      • M1: 2.25 → 1.35;
      • M2：2.11 → 1.27；
      • M3: 1.97 → 1.18;
      • M3 +：1.8 → 1.08
    • 雷暴炮’s "穿甲弹药":
      • 移除了后坐力惩罚
    • 镭射炮’s "快速射击模式”:
      • Now consumes 375 每次射击能量 instead of 380;
      • Additionally reduces the energy recovery rate after a shot by 15
  • 无人机 (all):
    • Now increase 炮塔伤害 and 底盘 defense by 1% to 5%
  • "驱动器" 无人机:
    • Recharge time is now 20 seconds instead of 12
  • 更新了对现有道具的效果 - 4月11日新增
    • Now, 维修工具, Double 伤害 (DD), Double Armour (DA), or 速度提升 have their respective visual effects when activated, which will show up on the 坦克 at any distance. This will provide valuable tactical and strategic information for the attentive 坦克手.

2018

11月3日（更新534）

  • 44 new 射击效果 added to the game for 火焰炮, 冰风暴, 磁力炮, 离子炮, 火龙珠, 火箭炮, 激光炮 and 镭射炮炮塔.
  • 改动平衡调整：
    • 火龙珠 alteration «狂暴»:
      • now when destroying an enemy restored 100% of the ammo 坦克, and not 25%.
    • 轰天炮改装 «自动加农炮»:
      • now reduces 伤害 by 85%, and not 75%;
      • 现在将后坐力降低了33%，而不是66%。
    • 极速炮更改 «燃烧带»:
      • 现在点燃目标，造成每秒 0.2 的伤害，而不是每秒 0.8；
      • additionally reduces 伤害 by 10%.
    • 雷暴炮改装 «“大锤” 弹药»:
      • 现在将炮弹重装时间减少30%，而不是20%.
    • 激光炮 alteration «不稳定轮环»:
      • now increases 最高伤害 by 90%, and not by 50%;
      • now reduces minimal 伤害 to 1 hp, and not to 5 hp.
    • 马格南改装 «迫击炮»:
      • now 地雷 placed by a shot is active for 30 seconds.
  • 在战斗中，为玩家在坦克上方的变化添加了指示。


10月31日（更新533）

  • 30 new gameplay alterations added to the game.
  • Changes to current alterations balance:
    • 火焰炮改装 «高压泵»:
      • 价格从50,000降到20,000；
      • 另外将最小命中距离增加 10%
    • 火焰炮 alteration «紧凑型坦克»:
      • 价格从100,000降至70,000；
      • now increases max. temperature by 200%, from 150%.
    • 冰风暴 alteration «高 pressure pump»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • additionally increases min. hit distance by 10%.
    • 磁力炮 alteration «宽带发射器»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • now reduces hit distance by 25%, from 30%.
    • 磁力炮 alteration «支援纳米机器人»:
      • price reduced from 100,000 to 55,000;
      • 现在，治疗模式下不再减少能耗，而是将治疗提高50%。
    • 离子炮 alteration «等离子体加速器»:
      • 价格从50,000降到20,000；
      • now reduces 炮弹重装时间 by 25%, from 20%.
    • 离子炮改造 «稳定等离子体»:
      • 价格从50,000降至45,000；
      • additionally increases strength of impact and 后坐力 by 10%.
    • 轰天炮改装 «突击弹药»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • 现在将冲击强度从30%提高到35%。
    • 极速炮 alteration «更快速的水平跟踪»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • 现在将炮塔旋转的减速从70%降低到50%.
    • 雷暴炮改造 «穿甲弹药»:
      • 价格从50,000降到20,000；
      • additionally increase strength of impact and 后坐力 by 10%.
    • 激光炮改造 «更快速的水平跟踪»:
      • 价格从50,000降到20,000；
      • 现在将转向灵活度从35%提高40%。
    • 激光炮改造 «稳定轮环»:
      • price reduced fromо 100,000 to 35,000;
      • additionally retains 启动加速度 of the shot through targets by 100%.
    • 激光炮改装 «大口径弹药»:
      • 此外，将射击前的延迟增加20%。
    • 镭射炮改造 «重型电容器»:
      • price reduced from 50,000 to 20,000;
      • now increases min. 伤害 by 20%, from 25%;
      • now increases 炮弹重装时间 by 25%, from 20%.
  • 游戏中已移除租用改装的选项。
  • 游戏玩法的改变现在根据等级解锁，而不是炮塔的改装。
  • Now only one gameplay alteration can be 装备 for each 炮塔.
  • 现在炮塔射击的标准颜色不依赖于其改装。


October 30 (Update 532)

  • 任务 system reworked:
    • 任务 chains 被替换为每周任务。
    • Added new 幸运礼盒 type — 每周任务礼盒.
      • 每周任务礼盒 includes a set of bonuses: 水晶 and 道具.
      • 每周任务礼盒 can be earned only as a 奖励 for completing 每周任务.
    • Added new types of 每日任务:
      • 在战斗中激活过速装置；
      • finish 战斗;
      • finish 战斗 in specific 模式.
    • 作为任务奖励的3倍VIP小时数已从游戏中移除。
    • “Collect 道具” 任务 can now be completed by activating specific 道具.
    • 稍微增加了更改每日任务的费用。
  • 9 new 无人机 added for purchase in the 车库.
  • 3 new 无人机套件 added to the 商店:
    • «Trinity» — «供应», «守卫者», «奔跑者» 无人机;
    • «无人机 amid a clear sky» — «魔术师», «助推器», «救生员» 无人机;
    • «Full house» — «破坏者», «露营者», «爆破手» 无人机.
  • In the «Second coming» 套件 the «供应» 无人机 was replaced with the new «工兵» 无人机.
  • 无人机平衡的变化：
    • 突袭:
      • changed bonus for the 持续时间 of active 道具:
        • 没有升级: (7 → 3), 秒.
      • 充能时间从10秒增加到12秒。
    • 驱动器:
      • 更改了每摧毁一辆敌方坦克时过速装置充能减少的时间量：：
        • 完全升级：(20 → 30)，秒/击杀。
      • recharge reduced from 15 to 12 seconds.
    • 工程师:
      • recharge increased from 5 to 10 seconds.
    • 供应:
      • 现在可以从上尉等级购买，而不是WO5；
      • 价格从 50,000 增加到 90,000 水晶。

  • Changed the geometry of the 匹配 version of 广场3C.


7月20日（更新518）

  • A new “剑圣” 模式 added to the game (available from the 上士等级).
  • 一份更新版的演练场地图已被添加到匹配地图列表中。
  • 平原地图匹配版本的额外更新。
  • 维修工具道具现在可以从新兵等级购买。
  • 地雷道具 now available for purchase from the 下士等级.
  • 双倍护甲和双倍伤害道具现在可以从中士等级购买。
  • 战斗 List of PRO-战斗 and PRO 解锁星级挑战奖励加成 now available from 五级准尉.
  • 炮塔平衡的变更：
    • 雷暴炮:
      • slightly reduced 炮弹重装时间;
      • 大大增加了最高伤害的距离；
      • 稍微增加了最小伤害的距离；
      • 稍微降低了射击的启动加速度的影响；
      • increased the 启动加速度 of the 溅射 explosion;
      • added new parameters “射程 of average impact” and “percentage of average impact”.
    • 镭射炮:
      • slightly reduced the recharge time between shots while NOT in Sniper 模式;
      • slightly increased the 最高射程 of shots NOT in Sniper 模式.
      • reduced by two times the 射程 of minimal impact of shots while NOT in Sniper 模式;
      • reduced by two times the percentage of weak impact shots while NOT in Sniper 模式;
      • the amount of 每次射击能量 slightly reduced, and the parameter is no longer upgradable.


June 30 (Update 516)

  • 每日任务获得经验值被替换为战斗中获得分数的任务。
  • Fixed error in 匹配 when several 战斗小组 could be put onto the same 团队, and at the same time no 战斗小组 would be placed on the opposing 团队.
  • The number of 玩家报告 required for the 战斗 to be highlighted for 战斗 moderators to check was lowered from 25% to 15% of the number of 玩家 in the 战斗.


6月23日（更新515）

  • Balance changes in 炮塔:
    • 冰风暴 — 伤害 increased on all modifications:
      • М0: 375 → 529;
      • М1: 488 → 647;
      • М2: 533 → 706;
      • М3: 669 → 882;
      • М3+: 760 → 1000.
  • 磁力炮 — 移除了能解冻和熄火坦克的能力。
  • Balance changes in 无人机:
    • 突袭 — increased bonus to the active time for 道具:
      • 未经修改：(5 → 7)，秒；
      • 完全升级：(10 → 15)，秒
    • 骑兵 — increased the active time of 道具:
      • 未经修改：(7 → 10)，秒；
      • fully upgraded: (15 → 20), sec.
    • Mechanic — increased 治疗半径:
      • without modifications: (10 → 15), meters;
      • fully upgraded: (20 → 25), meters.
  • 更改了多个出生点、基地和旗子的职务，在地图亚历山大罗夫斯克、路桥大战、工厂之战、大桥3C、德国小镇、广场3C、2042的匹配版本中。

  • Updated 迷彩 descriptions for “Champion”, “Silver”, “Bronze”, “Acid” and “Gladiator”.
  • 伊拉克和巴勒斯坦被加入到军团选择国家的名单中。

July 12 (Update 469)

  • New feature - “过速装置” added to the game.
    • 这个过速装置会为你和附近的队友激活所有5个道具（除金箱子之外）；
    • “过速装置 ON/OFF” option added to 专家战场设置;
    • 过速装置 is turned off by default in 格式战斗, except 跑酷.
  • Changes to 维修工具 mechanic:
    • 最初，维修工具立即恢复1000点生命值并减少着火和冷冻效果，然后在3秒内额外恢复3000点生命值；
    • The repair-over-time effect will be interrupted if any 伤害 is sustained;
    • The repairing effect will be interrupted as soon as the 坦克 is fully repaired.
  • Changes to 道具 active/冷却 times:
    • 维修工具
      • 持续时间: 3 秒
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • Double 护甲
      • 持续时间：30秒
      • 冷却：30秒
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • Double 伤害
      • 持续时间：30秒
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • 速度提升
      • 持续时间: 30 seconds
      • 冷却: 30 seconds
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
    • 地雷
      • 伤害: Unchanged
      • 冷却：30秒
      • Smart 冷却: Reduced by 50%
  • 被摧毁坦克消失延迟和重生时间的变化：
    • Destroyed 坦克 disappearing delay time reduced from 3.5 sec to 1.5 sec
    • Respawn delay time increased from 2 sec to 4 sec
  • New 声音 and effects for 道具 panel.
  • Now you will be able to see the amount of hit points restored by friendly 磁力炮 or with picked up 维修工具.
  • Changing 迷彩 while being in a 战斗 now doesn’t cause immediate self-destructing.
    • New 迷彩 applies only after next respawn.
  • New key bindings for 过速装置 and 快速进入车库 added to 设置.
    • Now you will be able to open 车库 while being in a 战斗 by pressing a key.
  • Fixed bugs in “Odnoklassniki” app.

  • 暴击错误已禁用：

January 26 (Update 436)

    • First iteration of 军团 system.
    • Released with limited functionality.
  • Changes in 火龙珠 mechanics:
    • Number of shots in 弹匣 increased from 12 to 14.
    • Vertical 瞄准 angle decreased.
    • 射程 of 最高伤害 is increased.
  • 轰天炮:
    • Decreased 射击速度.
    • Decreased 暴击伤害.
  • User Interface - When clicking on the 车库 button during a 战斗, 玩家 will no longer be asked whether they want to leave the 战斗, and will instead be taken directly to the 车库 without leaving the 战斗.

11月16日（更新426）

  • Implemented system for managing multiple 账号 on login
  • Implemented “战斗” button for Quick 战斗. The button will automatically send the 玩家 to a 战斗 on that 服务器 that best fits that 玩家’s 等级. Please note that this system:
    • doesn't work for 专家战场 (ignores them).
    • sends 玩家 only to recently started 战斗.
    • sends 玩家 to 地图 that are closer to being full.
    • doesn't evaluate 玩家装备 or 能力.
  • Non-VIP and Non-Pro 解锁星级挑战奖励加成 users now can only create 15min 战斗.
  • Fixed issues with Paysafecard.
  • Fixed 冰风暴 bug, where 坦克 is still frozen after respawn.
  • Fixed bug with 狮子 T-B M3 incorrectly displaying 46% 离子炮抗性 instead of 50% in 战斗.
  • Time of inactivity before kick has been decreased to 120 Seconds.
  • The time for autofinish to become active has been decreased to 180 seconds.
  • The Autofinish timer has now been decreased to 30 seconds.

2011

October 17

  • Amendments made to the «镭射炮» gun.


September 23

  • The incorrect display of «镭射炮» performance in the 车库 has been fixed. All purchased guns have been removed, and the 水晶 paid for them refunded.
  • A new 地图 was added -«Labyrinth» .
  • In the list of tips that appear when loading a game, a new recommendation— «Do not talk.»


September 22

  • 镭射炮 gun re-balancing was finished. Previous version of the gun was confiscated from all 玩家 who bought it and spent 水晶 were repaid.
  • In new version of the gun we:
    • simplified 控制;
    • added possibility to 射击 without using 辽源;
    • added possibility to stay in sniper 模式 as long as you want with fully charged gun;
    • removed black filling in 辽源模式;
    • visually enhanced the 辽源;
    • changed 箱子 and 旗子 displaying in 辽源模式, now they become semitransparent to simplify 瞄准.
    • Four new 迷彩 added to the 车库: Irbis, Jade, Lead, Needle
    • added new 地图公路大战 from MonkeyMagic.


September 9

  • 我们在第一个战斗界面添加了“注册”按钮。现在新玩家可以注册，而不必完成第一次战斗。用户仍然可以在第一次战斗或任何其他战斗中获得第一级别并获取奖励。
  • 密码长度被限制为32个符号。


9月1日

  • 使用Paypal支付水晶的服务已恢复。
  • The cost of all payments through SMS are now include VAT.
  • The 最低 payment through SMS payment for MTC subscribers has been set at 300 roubles. This change was made by the service provider itself. In the past an error could be experienced when attempting to make a payment less than 300 roubles.
  • The ability to make a one symbol 密码 without an 电子邮件 has been excluded.


8月25日

  • 注册表格已经改进了。它变得更小、更方便——更好看了。
  • 战斗 creation has been optimized for newbies, thanks to that fact in such 战斗 there will be more 玩家.
  • In the loading screen «TV grid» has been replaced with the game logo.


August 18

  • We have changed the formula of user rating calculating. Now it doesn’t count 水晶 bought for real money. The rating of all users will be recalculated in two days.
  • We have simplified the game entering mechanics. Now after clicking the Start

button a newcomer enters the 战斗 without registration. There he can meet 坦克手 of 新兵, 二等兵 and 一等兵等级. Such a 玩家 automatically gets the 昵称 RecruitNNNNN, where NNNNN is unique number.

  • A 玩家 is offered to fill the registration form only after

reaching 二等兵等级.

  • If you are not a newcomer, but also found yourself in a 战斗 with newbies and with 昵称 RecruitNNNNN, then click «I have an 账号» button in the upper part of the game menu. We have created a basic achievement system, which 帮助 newcomers to learn some basic elements of the game. Now you get 水晶 prizes for such actions, as registration after the first 战斗, joining the first 战斗 after registration, first buying in the 车库 etc.
  • We have changed loading indications. Now it looks like the charging

火炮的机械结构。同时，在加载过程中会显示游戏建议。

  • 我们已经简化了注册表格。
  • The Tab button now is functional in all fields.
  • 您只需输入较少的信息即可注册。只需昵称和

密码是必填项。

  • 名人堂按钮已从游戏菜单中移除。
  • 现在每个玩家都可以在没有通行证的情况下创建无道具战斗。

创建者也可以在没有通行证的情况下进入这场战斗。

  • We have improved the WebMoney payment option. Now you can choose the

在付款部分直接显示货币和水晶数量。

  • The 镭射炮 gun became visually shorter.
  • We have created a 特殊迷彩 for moderators.
  • 玩家 notification regarding the Double 水晶 bonus card was

optimized.

  • If a 玩家 has such a card, he sees an alternative version of the 购买

button.

  • The sum on the Add button in the 车库 is adjusted for Double

水晶.

  • Notification about an active Double 水晶 bonus card is shown in

the payment section.

March 23

  • 新注册表格。


March 21

  • We have realized sources storage in local SharedObject of Flash 玩家. It 允许 us to abandon browser caching system, which is not very reliable. For example, sources could disappear from browser cache because of its limited 大小. Now sources are downloaded from the 服务器 only if they were changed. It can drastically reduce time of game loading.


March 4

  • 我们已经增强了反作弊系统。
  • We have installed 特殊 billboards, added Holiday 迷彩 to the 车库 and replaced 旗子 with the bouquets in 互夺军旗模式 in honour of International Women’s Day, which is celebrated on the 8th of March.
  • We have corrected the Nitro effect for the frozen 坦克. Now you will be better able to feel this effect.
  • Four new 服务器 are launched.

February 15

  • We connected new emitter for collecting VISA/MasterCard payments — Uniteller.
  • 我们更换了PayPal聚合器。现在我们通过OnlineDengi接受PayPal支付。
  • 独特的枪械轰天炮 XT 变得更强大了。现在它造成的伤害不是 16–36，而是 26–46 点伤害。此外，我们将轰天炮 XT 的炮弹冲击的启动加速度提高到了 2.2。
  • 我们修复了«Double 水晶»奖励卡概述。现在它包含以下信息：奖励水晶在推荐转账中不会计入账号，在过渡到3D坦克2.0时，它们将像普通水晶一样计算，但不像已购买的水晶。

  • We’ve added new item in your 每日 presents — the «Double 水晶» discount card. This card 允许 you to get double your money’s worth for 水晶.

  • 我们稍作优化，进一步降低了卡顿的风险。
  • The 服务器 restart schedule has been changed. 服务器 1–7 will restart at 15:00 (UTC +3) with evacuation to 服务器 8–12.
  • We’ve redesigned the «购买» button, giving it a fresh look.
  • The Chronopay payment system has been temporarily turned off. Our aggregator no longer works with Chornopay, but we are in the process of establishing a direct relationship with Chronopay.
  • 我们已经消除了Izidia射击效果中的错误。
  • We’ve enhanced the droplist in 战斗 creation.
  • We’ve solved the problem that occurred when a 玩家 would gain 1,000,000 points during a 战斗, but would not achieve the Marshall 等级 until they re-entered the 战斗.
  • We’ve also solved the problem of when 道具 icons blinking even after the effect of the 道具 was over.


2月3日

  • 导致所谓“不可见字符”出现的一个错误已被消除
  • 所有的新年装饰品，包括圣诞树（已取代旗子）、节日降落伞、包装礼物以及节日主题的广告牌，都已被移除。

  • 车库已经通过渐进加载进行优化。进入车库时，只有可见的物品会被加载，从而加快进入速度。所有其他信息将在玩家滚动物品列表时加载。
  • 我们已经推出了一个通知系统，当玩家达到新的等级时会立即通知他们。消息会在战斗中显示。
  • We have also launched an alert system, informing 玩家 about new items available for purchase in the 车库. A message displaying the icons of these items will appear when a 玩家 receives a new 等级 and leaves 战斗 or enters the game. Click on the icon guides to the description of the item in the 车库.


February 1

  • Overloaded database, caused game instability, was modified. Now all 玩家’s achievements are not only saved but also stored through Redis. This solves a lot of issues. Due to this update search logic in the Hall of Fame is temporarily changed. To find user, you should type his full 昵称, not part of it.

  • 电子邮件（密码）更改缺失字母的问题已解决。

January 26

  • 战斗 creation form was modified:
    • 下拉列表变长了；
    • 现在可以按地图名称的首字母进行搜索；
    • the last chosen 地图 is saved in memory.
  • 坦克, whose sources weren't completely loaded, are marked with grey color in 战斗统计数据 (press «Tab» to call it). This 帮助 to solve problem of incomplete sources loading and resists to so-called «invisibles».
  • 互夺军旗模式中出现错误，导致一些延迟，已被消除。
  • 错误信息现在更详细。这有助于更快地发现和解决问题。
  • Hash for 服务器 entering without 密码 during evacuation and hash for permanent 服务器 entering without 密码 are differ now. It increases 防护等级 of the game.


January 18

  • No-道具战斗中用于奖励管理的按钮已恢复。在按钮缺失期间购买了 No-道具战斗通行证的玩家，已返还他们的水晶。
  • 加载器图片已更改。
  • Payments check system now sends letters to users from 上将 tech support 电子邮件 address 帮助@tankionline.com. It means you can contact technical support 团队 to get info about your request just by answering received 电子邮件.


January 2

  • 防护 system from hash pickup was enhanced. Generating algorithm was changed, time between trials to enter by hash was increased. Besides, all 坦克手 entering the game will get new hash automatically.


January 1

  • 新地图: «空中楼阁» 作者 Flanagun 和 «山谷» 作者 123egor
  • 冬天来到了地图 «孔贝», «小岛», «小方块», «城堡争夺» 和 «黑色城堡»
  • Payment bug 报告 system was upgraded. Now when 玩家 sends payment bug 报告, system automatically checks if this payment was successful or not. If it was, 玩家 receives confirmation letter. If it wasn’t, tech support 团队 automatically gets task and 玩家 receives a letter about that. Note: if 玩家 made a few identical payments, it is necessary to specify that in payment bug 报告 form.

October 18

  • 坦克 is no longer a barrier for 冰风暴 or 火焰炮 streams.
  • If you were forcibly disconnected from 服务器 you can not connect to this 服务器 for 5 minutes. But you can connect to any 其他服务器 immediately.
  • «Phantom» problem is solved. Earlier, if user disconnected during loading he became so called «phantom». He was in the list of 战斗 but he wasn’t in the game.
  • Added 备用镜头 behaviour which slightly improves view under 低 ceilings by pitching 镜头 up. To turn on the 模式 check «备用镜头 behaviour» option in the 设置 dialog.

September 29

  • Setting of mip-mapping turn-on(off) function, which will bring down picture quality, but will raise performance and reduce the use of working memory. View the demo with mip-mapping function here (use 宇宙 to turn on/off).
  • Eliminated vulnerabilities which led to the following problems: destroyed or invisible 坦克 which could 射击 and move.


September 27

  • «Hall of Fame " was transported to a separate 服务器. This improvement solved the problem with uneven achievement changes in hall of fame, raised game 服务器' performance and speeded 服务器' restarts greatly, but there will be a delay with rate 升级 (up to 15 minutes).
  • Now the 大小 of activated and gathered first-aid 套件 is summed up.
  • Eliminated vulnerabilities which led to the following troubles: 道具' re-use; 坦克' acceleration.


August 26

  • We have made traffic encryption. Cheat users are detected. They will be fined to 25% of all achievements, 水晶 on the 账号 and stuff in the 车库.
  • Client side of the game was optimized to solve some problems with game performance.
  • 新外套（Taiga、Cedar、Clay、Sandstone、Rock、Prodigi）。
  • 火龙珠 was rebalanced. All early bought 火龙珠 put out from the 车库 and 水晶 for them returned.
  • 冰风暴 was rebalanced. Now 冰风暴伤害 victim from the beginning and 冰风暴 it at the same time.
  • 聊天 was split in Russian and English versions.
  • New function in the 聊天: deleting 聊天 history by 玩家’s 昵称.
  • The problem with cutting off hanged up 玩家 is solved.
  • The 质量 and dynamics of 蜂王 M3 was restored.
  • 碰撞时坦克跳动的问题已解决。
  • 磁力炮瞄准 priority was changed. If ally has full health 磁力炮 doesn't detect it as an aim.
  • Time checking system for resource loading was added. If resources can not be loaded for certain time the loading will be started from the beginning.
  • Bonus medkit value is changed. Now the medkit found during 战斗 heals 50% of 底盘 HP.
  • Appearance of different 冰风暴 modifications now differs.
  • The problem of displaying previews which don’t correspond to 地图 was solved.
  • Now the 大小 of explosion depends on the 大小 of 坦克.

When you click this button you get the 电子邮件 with the link forwarding you to the page with the form for 电子邮件 and 密码 changing. If you didn’t specify an 电子邮件 you can make changes right in the 设置 menu without confirmation.

  • 已添加公共秩序 #论坛 — 切换到论坛。
  • Fixed bugs with 密码 and 电子邮件 change in 设置.
  • 现在邀请好友获得的额外水晶可以在«Invitation 统计数据»按钮上查看。
  • 修复了水晶接收邀请好友时的错误。他们今天将会被计算在内。


March 30

  • First stage of 服务器 optimization has been finished. Lags should reduce. Lags are network latencies during which 坦克 switch 职务, bonuses and 旗子 are taken with delay.


March 19

  • Now the distance between a 旗子 carrier and the base is taken into 账号 during 水晶 calculation for 旗子 return in 互夺军旗.
  • Now bug 报告 can be sent by testers only. If you have a problem with payment, fill in the form and send a message from payment section. All 其他 problems and questions are discussed at 论坛.
  • Now 火焰炮 and 猎人中甲 modifications look differently.
  • Now 火焰炮 modifications have different colour of the fire.
  • Coats were rebalanced (Swamp + 2% from 离子炮 (total 15%); Safari + 5% from 轰天炮; Dragon + 5% from 磁力炮; Roger + 5% from 激光炮; Jaguar — 10% from 火焰炮, но +5% from 激光炮 and +5% from 磁力炮; Electra +5% from 激光炮).
  • Added new 地图 with new props 炼油厂保卫战.
  • 地图 which used to be available to 低等级 are now available for higher ones also: 训练场 II, 演练场 II and 小桥之战 II.
  • New orders appeared (#等级 — switch to 论坛 topic «等级», #军团 — switch to 论坛 thread «军团»).


March 10

  • Experimentally reduced points for 磁力炮 cure. Coefficient was reduced from 2 to 1,5. Experiment will last for a week.


March 5

  • Button «Improve» is placed next to «Set» in the 车库.
  • Every modification of 炮塔 and shells is described now in a 特殊 table which is placed in the 车库.
  • Fixed bugs in 火焰炮 and 磁力炮: 火焰炮 had greater 伤害 effect than it had to, 磁力炮 had less 伤害 effect than it had to. Now similar modifications of 火焰炮 and 磁力炮 have equal 伤害 effect in full charge.
  • Fixed bug when 火焰炮 effect during 射击 while moving was displayed incorrectly. There used to be very long flame while moving backwards and very short one — while moving forward.
  • Abolished 通行证 — Double 分数. All the 玩家 who purchased the 通行证 during making changes on 服务器 will get their 水晶 back.
  • A new 通行证 was added — 分数 multiplier 通行证: multiplies all received points by 25%, lifetime — one month.
  • A new 通行证 was added — No-道具战斗: enables you to create and enter no-道具战斗, lifetime — one month.
  • Modifications of 激光炮 and 离子炮 look differently now.
  • Now the 地雷 is included in everyday present.


February 10

  • Added new consumable — 地雷. View details in FAQ.
  • Done effects visualization. View details in FAQ.
  • Changed visualization of consumable blocking time after usage (冷却).
  • Improved automatic anti-foul 语言 system: now the 聊天 knows 1 300 000 Russian words. If you do not misspell the words, false responses will be 珍奇.
  • Improved registration form — added check-up of nick availability (after you enter the needed nick and are inactive in entry field for two seconds or switching to 密码 entry field, the nick is checked and next to it you see a tick or a red 十字路口).
  • Now you get twice as much points for curing the 坦克手 who carries a 旗子.
  • Summer is back! All the 地图 now have pleasant green landscape.
  • 地图黑色城堡 and 城堡争夺 are back.
  • Added new 地图核电站 from Duke 2.0
  • Lessened 大厅 loading time due to reduction of loaded 地图 preview, now they load when needed.
  • Now every modification of 轰天炮, 火焰炮, 离子炮 and 激光炮 has own 图形 effect.
  • Now you can use alternative payment system for VISA/MasterCard in payment section.
  • Solved bug when points were not accounted when you kill 磁力炮 owner or a patient during cure.


January 22

  • Finally accepted modification of 离子炮: 垂直角度 of 瞄准 increased greatly (two degrees up, one down), lowered 速度 of bullets, finally accepted 伤害
  • Introduced paid 战斗 with no consumables.
  • Fixed bug when a consumable timer is stopped up after getting bonus.
  • Karma was introduced in 聊天: if you misbehaved, the 聊天 remembers it and takes into 账号 when giving automatic ban, but soon forgets about misbehaviour.
  • All newcomers will appear in the 战斗 at once without entering game menu.
  • Now you can invite 好友 to the game through email.
  • Payment systems Yandex. Dengi and Webmoney were moved to another payment aggregator (2Pay). But you still can pay through the former aggregator (OnlineDengi).
  • Now if you, for some 原因, lost connection with the game (being in the 战斗), you can return without loosing your achievements. Time to return into the 战斗 — 2 minutes.
  • Changed algorithm of anti-foul 语言 system. Within some period of time there can be false responses, since we’re perfecting the system. If you have examples of false responses please send them to 帮助@tankionline.com
  • Changed algorithm of anti-flood system, now anti-flood 关注 typing of similar symbols in a row in one message.
  • 旗子 finally have taken their stand.
  • Fixed bug of mismatch between number of 玩家 in the 战斗 list and 战场信息 (9/11).
  • Changed the 声音 of 离子炮 shooting.


January 16

  • Experimental changes in the 离子炮 gun: the 垂直角度 for automatic targeting is now increased (3 degrees upwards, 3 downwards), 速度 of flight of the individual shells is lowered.


January 14

  • Eliminated a vulnerability that allowed to increase the 速度 in 战斗 (aka 速度 hack). Now if you somehow 速度 up the 坦克, you’ll be automatically kicked from the 战斗.


January 12

  • 离子炮 is experimentally strengthened for one week. You can discuss the current 统计 and post your impressions/suggestions here
  • The referral banned display problem is now solved.
2009

December 31

  • It’s the New Year’s eve, and all the guns have gone crazy!


December, 30

  • 修复了磁力炮的治疗技能的问题。以前，治疗按百分比计算，而不是按生命值计算。
  • Added an option to enable/disable the 战斗聊天. If the combat 聊天 is turned off, messages will not be displayed. However, you may press enter to view all the messages you missed as well as to write one yourself.


December 29

  • 更换了支付终端的聚合器。现在我们通过四个国家的终端接收支付
  • Redesigned section for 水晶 purchasing
  • Improved ban system
  • Added new SMS-payment aggregator. Now we receive payments in 67 countries


December 25

  • Fixed bug with automatic naming of 战斗 creation
  • Changed #plans, #faq и #rules considering new 论坛
  • Improved 阴影 under buildings on the snow
  • 到新论坛的链接会自动变为可点击的链接
  • Changed tree-旗子 design


December 23

  • 冬天来到了所有的地图
  • 旗子暂时被变成了杉树
  • 引入了自动将大写字母变为小写字母的系统
  • Fixed bug of damaging through walls with the 帮助 of 火焰炮
  • The principle of 暂停模式 has been changed. The 暂停模式 is activated by pressing P or 暂停 button. If a 坦克 has been destroyed while 暂停 is active, the 坦克 doesn’t spawn until the 暂停模式 is disabled. In the beginning of a new round all 坦克 are spawned regardless of active 暂停.
  • In 聊天 when entering #plans appears conversion into clickable link to the corresponding 论坛 thread. in 聊天 #plans is displayed as Задачи и планы разработчиков in Russian localization and Developers’ 任务 and plans in English one
  • 地图城堡争夺和 黑色城堡暂时断开连接以准备过冬


12月18日

  • 在聊天中，输入 #faq 或 #rules 时会转换为可点击的链接，指向相应的论坛主题。在聊天中，#faq 在俄语和英语本地化中显示为 FAQ，而 #rules 在俄语本地化中显示为 Правила，在英语本地化中显示为 Rules
  • In 聊天 the links to the 论坛 are clickable
  • Own 坦克 doesn’t have now nick and 等级 indication next to health/charge indication stripes
  • Fixed bug of single-use items use of a 坦克 in inactive (translucent) 模式
  • 修复了在满血状态下急救包只能使用一次的错误
  • Added new 地图: 十字路口 from eras, 混乱城市 from DJ_Efreitor, 城堡争夺 from GrUm, 黑色城堡 from GrUm, 山城大战 from DJ_Efreitor.

August 7

  • Added 聊天 orders to 禁止 messages from users:
    • /禁止 name – 禁止 messages from the 玩家 (works in 大厅 and 战斗聊天).
    • /unblock name – resume messages from 玩家 (works in 大厅 and 战斗聊天).
    • /blocklist – view the list of blocked 玩家 (works in 大厅).
    • /unblockall – clear the list of blocked 玩家 (works in 大厅).

The list of blocked users is kept in Shared Objects, so if you enter the game from the 其他 computer – it won't work.

  • Improvements in 火焰炮

  • 大约50米——同样的伤害
